The appearance of the hotel is very normal, but I was surprised when I entered the lobby. First, a waiter immediately came to help with the luggage. This service is of five-star standard. He was waiting for check-in, and then directly delivered the luggage to the room. Besides, the front desk brother also upgraded the deluxe room to an executive room for free, which felt very good. Later, because I didnâ€™t like the bathtub in the room, the front desk brother upgraded it to a small suite for free, and the sense of check-in was instantly improved a lot. Then the suite had fruit and dessert service, which made me feel good again. The key point is that there is also a room cleaning service before going to bed. Two cleaning sisters will come to make the bed very warm. It is said to be a suite service. After this series of operations, there is a sense of butler service, which is really great. The surrounding transportation is also convenient. There is a subway entrance at the door, and you can reach various attractions in Guiyang, so I simply stayed for a few more nights. I am a bit of a germaphobe, but this hotel is definitely a five-star rating!
